   function onSearchSubmit(form) {
                if ($(form).find('.search-input').length > 0) $(form).find('.search-input').val($(form).find('.search-input').val().toLowerCase());
                else if ($(form).find('#search_input').length > 0) $(form).find('#search_input').val($(form).find('#search_input').val().toLowerCase());

    var numLatestArticlesInMenu = 15;

    function renderLatestArticlesInMenu(){
        var html = '';
        if(numLatestArticlesInMenu>0) {
            latestArticlesInMenu.forEach(function (category) {
                var elements = category.data;
                html += '<div class="hamburger-latest-articles ' + category.slug + '-hamburger-latest-articles">';
                html += '   <strong class="box-title">' + category.title + '</strong>';
                html += '   <ul>';
                elements.forEach(function (item) {
                    html += '       <li><a href="'+ item.slug + '" title="'+ item.title + '">'+ item.title + '</a></li>';
                });
                html += '   </ul>';
                html += '</div>';
            });

        }
        return html;
    }

    $( document ).ready(function() {
        $('#latestArticlesInMenu').parent().html( renderLatestArticlesInMenu() );
    });

      <script type="text/javascript">
       $(document).ready(function(){
                $(".userbox").click(function(event ){
                    $('.search-box-form, .middle-header .search-box-form').hide();

                    $(".middle-header").removeClass("active");
                    if ($(".userbox").hasClass("logged")) {
                        $(".user-info-header").hide();
                        $(".loggedGigya").show();
                    }
                    else
                    {
                        $(".user-info-header").show();
                        $(".loggedGigya").hide();
                    }
                    $(".userbox").toggleClass("activo");
                    $(".middle-header").addClass("active");
                    event.stopPropagation();
                });
                $(document).bind("click", function(){
                    if ($(".user-info-header").is(":visible") || $(".loggedGigya").is(":visible")){
                        $(".user-info-header").hide();
                        $(".loggedGigya").hide();
                        $(".userbox").removeClass("activo");
                        $(".middle-header").removeClass("active");
                    }
                });
            });
      </script>
